\\n219:     /**\\n220:      * Authorize an action based on the current set of ACLs.\\n221:      *\\n222:      * In order to know whether to allow or deny the action, we need to examine the ACLs\\n223:      * that apply to it. }\\n310:     }\\n311: \\n312:     private MatchingRule findAclRule(\\n313:         Set<KafkaPrincipal> matchingPrincipals,\\n314:         String host,\\n315:         Action action\\n316:     ) {\\n317:         // This code relies on the ordering of StandardAcl within the NavigableMap.\\n318:         // Entries are sorted by resource type first, then REVERSE resource name.\\n319:         // \\n219:     /**\\n220:      * Authorize an action based on the current set of ACLs.\\n221:      *\\n222:      * In order to know whether to allow or deny the action, we need to examine the ACLs\\n223:      * that apply to it. If any DENY ACLs match, the operation is denied, no matter how\\n224:      * many ALLOW ACLs match. If neither ALLOW nor DENY ACLs match, we return the default\\n225:      * result. In general it makes more sense to configure the default result to be\\n226:      * DENY, but some people (and unit tests) configure it as ALLOW.\\n227:      */\\n228:     public AuthorizationResult authorize(\\n229:         AuthorizableRequestContext requestContext,\\n230:         Action action\\n231:     ) {\\n232:         if (action.resourcePattern().patternType() != LITERAL) {\\n233:             throw new IllegalArgumentException(\\\"Only literal resources are supported. So log only at trace level.\\n292:                 if (action.logIfAllowed() && auditLog.isDebugEnabled()) {\\n293:                     auditLog.debug(buildAuditMessage(principal, requestContext, action, rule));\\n294:                 } else if (auditLog.isTraceEnabled()) {\\n295:                     auditLog.trace(buildAuditMessage(principal, requestContext, action, rule));\\n296:                 }\\n297:                 return;\\n298: \\n299:             case DENIED:\\n300:                 // logIfDenied is true if access to the resource was explicitly requested. Since this is an attempt\\n301:                 // to access unauthorized resources, log at info level. If false, this is either a request to determine\\n302:                 // authorized operations or a filter (e.g for regex subscriptions) to filter out authorized resources.\\n303:                 // In this case, log only at trace level.\\n304:                 if (action.logIfDenied()) {\\n305:                     auditLog.info(buildAuditMessage(principal, requestContext, action, rule));\\n306: {\\n317:         // This code relies on the ordering of StandardAcl within the NavigableMap.\\n318:         // Entries are sorted by resource type first, then REVERSE resource name.\\n319:         // Therefore, we can find all the applicable ACLs by starting at\\n320:         // (resource_type, resource_name) and stepping forwards until we reach\\n321:         // an ACL with a resource name which // For example, when trying to authorize a TOPIC resource named foobar, we would\\n326:         // start at element 2, and continue on to 3 and 4 following map:\\n327:         //\\n328:         // 1. exemplar.resourceName().substring(0, matchesUpTo),\\n415:                     exemplar.patternType(),\\n416:                     exemplar.principal(),\\n417:
